Subject: Request for withdrawal of notice issued to our PG premises and assurance of compliance
Respected Sir,
I am writing this letter with reference to the recent notice issued by the BBMP authorities at our Paying Guest (PG) / Co-Living premises Cozeevo Co-Living, located at No. 9B, 7th Cross Road, EP-IP Zone, Brookfield, Bengaluru – 560048, wherein our tenants have been asked to vacate due to the absence of certain trade licenses, documentation, and other required certificates.
I would like to respectfully submit that we are fully committed to complying with all BBMP rules, regulations, and statutory requirements applicable to PG / co-living establishments. We understand the importance of proper licensing and documentation, and we sincerely regret any oversight or delay from our side in completing the required procedures.
We assure you that we are ready to follow all the procedures as discussed and to obtain all the required trade licenses and certificates as prescribed by BBMP. We kindly request your guidance and cooperation to complete the compliance process in a timely and orderly manner.
In this regard, we humbly request you to kindly consider withdrawing the notice issued at our PG premises and allow us reasonable time to complete all the necessary formalities. Immediate vacation by tenants would cause significant hardship to them and operational difficulty for us, despite our genuine intention to regularize everything strictly as per BBMP norms.
We assure you of our full cooperation and strict compliance with all applicable rules and regulations going forward. We would be grateful for an opportunity to meet the concerned officials, if required, to clarify any additional requirements and ensure complete adherence.

📌 2) Section 23 of the CGST Act, 2017 — Exemption from Registration

Section 23 states:

A person exclusively making supply of non-taxable or wholly exempt goods or services is not liable to be registered under GST.

Explanation:

“Non-taxable” or “wholly exempt” supplies include transactions not subject to GST (like exempt rent) — so such a person need not obtain registration even if turnover is high ‎<This message was edited>
